                 <h2 class="story-title">
                  <a href="/article/us-health-coronavirus-biden/biden-orders-states-to-prioritize-vaccinations-for-teachers-sets-one-shot-target-by-end-march-idUSKCN2AU2ND" target="_self">
                   Biden confident there will be enough vaccines for every American by end of May
                  </a>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="byline">
                 </div>

        // Featured Module headings
const featured_headings = document.querySelectorAll('.featured-section .module-heading');

//Sponsor data array
const sponsors = new Array;

//Render container and push ad data to sponsors array
function renderSponsorContainer(id, type, el) {
	const sponsor_container = document.createElement('div');
	sponsor_container.id = id;
	sponsor_container.className = 'gpt-sponsored-mod';

	//Append container
	el.appendChild(sponsor_container);

	//Push to sponsors
	sponsors.push({
		el_id: id,
		ad_type: type
	});
}

// Check for keyowrds
for (i=0; featured_headings.length > i; i++) {
	const text = featured_headings[i].innerText.toLowerCase().trim();
	switch(text) {

		// LIFE LESSONS
		case 'life lessons':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorLifeLessons', 'llmodule', featured_headings[i]); 
			break;

		// BREAKINGVIEWS
		case 'breakingviews':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorBreakingviews', 'breakingviewsmodulelogo', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// TWITTER CHAT
		case 'twitter chat':
		case 'chats: reuters charity':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorChat', 'tc_module', featured_headings[i]);

		// EXCHANGE-TRADED FUNDS

			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorSectors', 'sector_module', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// INVESTING
		case 'investing':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorInvesting', 'investingmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// WORLD AT WORK
		case 'world at work':
                case 'the world at work':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorWorldAtWork', 'wowmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// AIRBUS
                case 'aerospace':
                case 'aerospace & defense':
		case 'farnborough airshow':
                case 'paris airshow':
                case 'paris air show':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorAirbus', 'airbusmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// DAVOS
                case 'davos':
		case 'davos coverage':
                case 'davos 2020':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorDavos', 'davmodule', featured_headings[i]);
			break;

		// FUTURE OF MONEY
		case 'future of money':
		case 'the future of money':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorFutureOfMoney', 'fom_hp_module', featured_headings[i]);
			break;
            
		// THE Z FACTOR
		case 'the z factor':
			renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorTheZFactor', 'zfac_hp_module', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// ESG
		case 'sustainable business':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorESG', 'esgmodule', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// FORWARD
		case 'forward':
		  	renderSponsorContainer('adSponsorForward', 'forwardmodule', featured_headings[i]);
		  	break;

		// MILKEN CONFERENCE
		case 'milken conference':
